Telegram from the National Postal Workers' Union Regarding the Number of Representatives to the National Assembly 120

The National Postal Workers' Union is sending a telegram to all relevant institutions and public organizations throughout the country, requesting them to uphold justice regarding the fact that "the number of representatives from the postal workers' union has not yet been stipulated in the National Assembly Representative Election Law." The telegram is addressed to: All ministries and departments of the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the governments of all provinces, cities, and counties, party headquarters at all levels, the General Office for the Election of Representatives to the National Assembly, all institutions and public organizations throughout the country, and compatriots from all walks of life: The National Assembly is the central hub of national public opinion. All members of the public should be able to elect representatives to participate in accordance with the law, so as to pool their wisdom and efforts to promote the constitution. Our postal workers' union has been established for more than ten years. All provinces, cities, and counties throughout the country have strict and sound organizations. Under the concrete guidance of the central and local party and government organs and the command and supervision of the National Postal Workers' Union, it has long made practical achievements for the party, the country, the postal service, and society. The facts are clear and need not be repeated. However, the National Assembly Representative Election Law and its implementing regulations promulgated by the Executive Yuan do not provide for the representation of the postal workers' union. Even special unions, such as railway and maritime workers, can participate as representatives, while the postal workers' union is excluded from the law. Such disregard for the revolutionary history and legal rights of 36,000 postal workers nationwide is not only a departure from the legislative fairness of the legislators themselves, but also something that our postal workers nationwide cannot remain silent about. Therefore, after deliberation by the National Postal Workers' Union, we have submitted a document to the National Government, the Military Affairs Commission, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Central Party Headquarters, and the General Office for the Election of Representatives to the National Assembly, requesting a revision of the number of representatives to show the sincere desire of the union to lead postal workers nationwide in supporting the constitution. The original submission is recorded below: "It has been found that according to the Implementing Rules of the National Assembly Representatives Election Law, only the railway and maritime unions are included as representatives of special unions, and the postal workers' union is completely excluded, which is perplexing and incomprehensible. Originally, it was based on the Organizational Regulations for Special Unions and the Organizational System Table for Special Unions promulgated by the 157th Standing Committee of the Second Session of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, and the 154th Central Standing Committee. We proceeded in accordance with them, which was in compliance with laws and regulations. Later, the Central Government cancelled the above-mentioned regulations and system table because the Trade Union Law had already been promulgated. The Association, in view of the precedents of the maritime and railway special unions, and in view of the fact that the Trade Union Law was not applicable to special unions, repeatedly suggested to the Central Training Department and the Legislative Yuan of the National Government in the 19th year of the Republic of China to promulgate a special trade union law, or the postal workers' union to hold an organizational law for compliance. On May 5th, the 20th year of the Republic of China, when the National Assembly was held, the Association, together with postal workers' unions in various places, united with representatives from various industrial circles to formally draft a proposal and submit it to the meeting. The Assembly decided that the case of promulgating the Special Trade Union Law should be submitted to the National Government for reference. At the First Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee, the Association sent representatives from trade unions along the Beijing-Shanghai Line to Beijing to petition and present detailed opinions to Zhongwei Ju Zheng, Wang Jingwei, Ye Chucang, Ma Chaojun, Zhang Zhiben, Chen Gongbo, Wang Qi, Fang Juehui, Wang Luyi, and other gentlemen, all of whom accepted them sincerely. After the reorganization of the People's Movement Association, Chen Gongbo, Chairman of the People's Movement Association, was in charge. With the summons of Chen, Director Chen Gongbo, and Wang, Deputy Director Wang Luyi, the two members Chen and Wang expressed the necessity of a general organization of trade unions, and said that the principle of organizing mass organizations was once mentioned by this person and passed by the First Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee, but the amendment of the Trade Union Law and the promulgation of the Special Trade Union Law still require time in terms of legal procedures. The People's Movement Association intends to formulate interim regulations within the possible scope to remedy them, etc. At the same time, the People's Movement Association instructed the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union (Original Order No. 229), etc., roughly stating, 'For information, after reviewing the documents, it was approved that the Central Secretariat sent a document to the association, etc., as a document requesting the rapid promulgation of the Special Trade Union Law and requesting that members be allowed to attend the meeting when drafting the law, with a draft of the Special Trade Union Law attached. According to this, the association is drafting the Special Trade Union Law in accordance with the recent decision of the Central Government to guide the mass movement plan. As for the request to allow members to attend the meeting when drafting the law, this association may send a letter of appointment when necessary. The draft of the Special Trade Union Law shall be retained for reference. In addition to distribution, please inform, etc.' It is clear that the Central Government attaches great importance to the postal workers' union. Until October of the 21st year of the Republic of China, the Executive Yuan promulgated the Organizational Rules of the Postal Workers' Union, but it has not been implemented because of some obstacles. It is too much to say that the establishment of the postal workers' union is not based on law. In short, the current organization of the postal workers' union is a sound group that can be driven by the party and the country. The facts show that it cannot be erased. At the beginning of the implementation of the constitution, this good social organization and this group that is beneficial to the party and the country should be supported by law to show the state's intention to maintain the people's movement. For the sake of society and the party and the country, we should promptly promulgate the Organizational Law of the Postal Workers' Union and approve the existing organization of the postal workers' union in accordance with the law to adapt to the needs of the facts and conform to the legislative purpose of the state. This is to continue the previous requests to promptly promulgate the Organizational Law of the Postal Workers' Union. It has been found that the postal workers' union is not included in the representatives of the National Assembly. The Association has previously consulted with the railway and maritime unions to submit petitions to the Central Party Headquarters, the Legislative Yuan of the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of the Interior, etc., requesting additional amendments, all of which have been approved for remediation in the implementing rules of the election law. It has now been found that the implementing rules of the election law have been promulgated. Although the railway and maritime unions have been included, the representatives of the postal workers' union are not specified, which is deeply alarming. If it is not to discriminate against the status of the postal workers' union, it is feared that it does not conform to the purpose of promoting the constitution. If it is said that the postal workers' union does not have a legal basis today and cannot be included as an example of representatives of the National Assembly, then the Association and the postal workers' unions in various places have been guided and trained by the party for many years, and have not been regarded as illegal organizations, but have been praised as models of trade unions. The existence of the postal workers' union today cannot be denied in fact. This is the first reason why the postal workers' union should not be excluded from the representatives of the National Assembly. It has been found that special trade unions were first created by the Prime Minister, and they have a large number of people and sound organizations. They have struggled for the revolution for many years and have contributed a lot to the party. The postal workers' union is one of the special trade unions, and its importance is no less than that of the railway and maritime unions. Moreover, from the standpoint of the party, it has a long history. Now that the railway and maritime unions have been included in the representatives of the National Assembly, and the postal workers' union has been excluded alone, who would say that this is fair? This is the second reason why the postal workers' union should be excluded from the representatives of the National Assembly. The party's ideology aims to achieve popular sovereignty, democracy, and people's ownership. On the eve of the implementation of the constitution, we are afraid that we will not be able to support and maintain the mass organizations and workers' movements. However, the postal workers' union has not received any support or maintenance from the beginning. It relies on self-reliance and takes the party's labor policy as its guide. The impact on the workers' movement in China is not insignificant. Furthermore, the postal workers' union has participated in the mass movements in various places, so the postal workers' union has not only become the center of the national labor movement, but also laid the foundation for the party's people's movement. Now that the trade unions of various industries and various mass organizations have been included in the representatives of the National Assembly, the postal workers' union, which has achieved remarkable results in the labor and people's movements, is not included, which is truly perplexing. This is the third reason why the postal workers' union should not be excluded from the representatives of the National Assembly. The above points are all based on facts. Therefore, we have listed the situation below. We implore you to promulgate and implement the organizational laws and regulations of the postal workers' union, and approve the existing organization of the postal workers' union in accordance with the law, and include the postal workers' union in the representatives of the National Assembly, and add the number of representatives to maintain postal operations and emphasize the constitution. We are eagerly awaiting orders." We hope that you will uphold justice and unanimously advocate for the achievement of our goals. Thank you. The National Postal Workers' Union of the Republic of China, July 10, 25th year of the Republic.

Hongxing Sock Factory: Refusal to Register Workers; Labor Union Requests Assistance from Du Yuesheng 124

The Hongxing Sock Factory on Caishi Road in the French Concession, due to the registration of workers and the indefinite work stoppage, caused panic among all the workers about their livelihoods. They petitioned the party and government agencies for relief. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned both parties to the bureau for questioning on Monday. It was decided that the factory should not dismiss workers, and the workers should all comply with the party and government-approved registration regulations to register with the factory. The factory was ordered to resume normal operations on the 20th of this month. However, yesterday morning, eight members of the factory's labor union went to the factory to register but were rejected. In addition to sending representatives to petition the party and government agencies, demanding that justice be upheld, they also appointed Zhang Zhuyun, Shi Xiuyun, Deng Yixin, and others to go to Du Yuesheng's residence with a written request yesterday afternoon, asking Mr. Du Yuesheng to provide assistance, and also requested Mr. Lu Jingshi, a member of the Municipal Party Department, to make a similar expression in order to maintain the livelihoods of hundreds of workers.

Two Overseas Chinese Encounter Scam Upon Arrival from the United States: Led to Hotel and Solicited Prostitutes for Company; Swindled Out of More Than Two Thousand US Dollars; Discovered the Next Morning, Reported to Police, and Arrested at Hotel 125

Li Xianjian and Lei Lin, both from Guangdong, have been engaged in business in the United States. Recently, they returned to China on the Empress of Canada, arriving at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Shanghai at 11 PM the night before. Because the ship had to stay in Shanghai for a day, Li and Lei went ashore to explore. At that time, Xie Daozhen, Shi Hong, and Liang Ji, all from Guangdong, stepped forward and offered to be their guides. Li and others were worried about being unfamiliar with the area, so they immediately hired them as guides. Xie then helped Li and Lei check into rooms 334 and 330 at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road for a temporary stay. Xie then encouraged Li and Lei to engage with prostitutes and solicited two prostitutes for them. Xie told Li and others that the prostitutes in Shanghai were of very low character and that it was dangerous for them to carry money. He claimed that he was an employee of the New Asia and could send all their money to the cashier's office for safekeeping. Li and Lei believed him. Li handed over all his US dollars, totaling 400, and eight checks, totaling 1700. Lei also handed over 240 US dollars to Xie, who issued two receipts before leaving. Yesterday morning at 4 AM, when Li and others wanted to retrieve the money, they went to the cashier's office at the New Asia to retrieve it. The cashier's office replied that they had not received the money. Li and Lei realized they had been scammed and told the whole story. The New Asia reported to the Hongkou Police Station. Under the investigation of Chinese Detective Chen Xikang, Xie Dehua, a room attendant from room 198 of the New Asia, stated that he had seen Xie Daozhen go to room 411. The detectives went to that room and found Xie, Shi, and Liang inside. All three were arrested. In the room, they also found Lu Guinian, Zhao Min, Li Xing, Cai Shan, and four other Cantonese. All the original stolen goods were found under the pillow. Three banknotes from the Zhobian Bank, which had been closed for more than ten years, were found on the ground, totaling twenty yuan. All were taken back to the police station. At 9 AM, they were escorted to the Fifth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu prosecuted them for defrauding under Article 339 of the Criminal Law, stating that this kind of incident was currently occurring, and the defendant Shi Hong had been sent to the court by the police station for a similar incident, but he was released due to insufficient evidence because the victim did not stay long and returned to Guangdong. Due to the urgency of the time, a detailed investigation had not yet been conducted, so they requested an adjournment for further questioning. Judge Ye Shengchao briefly questioned Li, Lei, and the defendants, then announced an adjournment. The recovered stolen goods were returned to the plaintiff.

Rapid Floodwater Recession Relieves Yangtze River Concerns: Hankou Retreats to Below Thirty Feet; Water Levels in Jiujiang and Wuhu Fall Consistently 126

Since the Yangtze River flooded, the downstream areas, such as Hankou, reached a high of 35 feet 5 inches, only 3 feet 3 inches lower than the high water level during the major flood of 1931. Therefore, the situation was very serious. Fortunately, the water levels have since receded. Although fluctuations have been observed recently, none have exceeded 35 feet. As of the 12th of this month, according to the Hankou water level report received by the customs, it has receded to below 30 feet, measured at 29 feet. The water level in Jiujiang on the same day also receded to 32 feet (36 feet 4 inches on the 1st of this month). The water level in Wuhu on the same day also receded to 20 feet 9 inches (23 feet on the 1st of this month). Observing the above water levels, they are consistently falling, and the retreat is very rapid. From now on, the Yangtze River basin may be able to celebrate peace.

National Products Exhibition Scheduled to Open 127

The North Shanghai National Products Exhibition will open on the 17th, the Special District National Products Exhibition will open on the 20th, and the West Shanghai National Products Exhibition is scheduled to hold a lantern parade on the 26th. The details are summarized as follows:

North Shanghai

The North Shanghai National Products Exhibition was delayed due to the incomplete amusement park construction, so only the business was opened on the 11th. Now that the construction is complete, the association has specially invited famous figures in drama, storytelling, and opera to open at 2 PM on the 17th, following the opening ceremony. Shan Wangxiaolai will unveil the curtain, and Wang Manyun will raise the flag. At the same time, people from all walks of life in the city will be invited, and gifts will be given to the guests.

West Shanghai

The Shanghai West Shanghai National Products Exhibition has been very popular since its opening, with many visitors from all walks of life. More than 60 factories are participating in the exhibition, which is divided into two sections: display and temporary market. The display section has been arranged and officially opened. The goods sold in the temporary market are all exquisite national products and daily necessities for the summer. Because the association first promotes national products and encourages people to try them, the prices are particularly low and suitable for the common people in the factory area of West Shanghai. However, in order to maintain costs, each factory has regulations and restrictions on the purchase of goods by guests. All the facilities of the association are meticulous and thoughtful. All the on-site staff are dispatched at any time, and they answer questions from guests sincerely. The factory staff can also follow the rules and treat people with courtesy. Therefore, although the large venue is bustling and noisy, the order is well-maintained. According to the association's statistics, about 14,200 visitors have attended in the five days since the opening, and the business in the market has reached more than 9,800 yuan. The exact figures will be published after detailed statistics in a week. In addition, the association plans to hold a lantern parade, which is actively being prepared and is scheduled to be held on the 26th.

Special District

The Special District National Products Exhibition is scheduled to open on the 20th. Yesterday, a meeting of factory representatives was held, attended by more than 40 people. Jiang Shangen chaired the meeting. The following resolutions were made: (1) The association should appoint famous figures in the national products industry to form a committee to expand the association. It was resolved to appoint Wang Xiaoxiang, Yuan Ludeng, Lin Kanghou, Zhu Gengtao, Zhou Bangjun, Xu Xiaochu, Le Zhoucheng, Qian Zongjian, Xu Genghua, Jiang Shangen, Xu Yunhui, Wang Hanqiang, Lin Guyun, Shen Liucun, and Xu Jianruo as members. (2) The association should appoint publicity committee members to expand publicity efforts. It was resolved to appoint Tao Leqin, Zhu Yutao, Ge Futian, Zheng Dongshan, Wang Zhaobi, Sun Baohui, Zhu Bin, Li Peiying, Cheng Gengnong, Yan Yongqing, and others as publicity committee members. A letter was also sent to various factories: "Dear Sirs, at a time when international tensions are increasing, the whole country is striving for self-reliance as a way to solve problems, and the national products movement is the basic work of self-reliance. If we can work together with one heart and mind and actively carry out this movement, the revival of the national economy and the revitalization of national industry can be expected soon. In view of this, our association has surveyed and determined that the former site of the Zhonghua Xingye Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Shili Road (more than a dozen city houses, including all the rooms on the second floor) will hold the "Shanghai Special District National Products Exhibition," dividing the venue into 80 rooms and soliciting participation from national products manufacturers. The exhibition will last for one month and is scheduled to open on the 20th of this month. The location is central and the transportation is convenient, making it the most prosperous area in the city. With a grand scale and effective publicity, the business prospects can be assured. We have always admired your factory's excellent products, which bring glory to national products. Therefore, we are sending this letter to solicit your participation to promote publicity and support the grand event. There are not many venues, so please register as soon as possible to avoid being left out when the quota is full."

Statistics on Registered Opium Smokers Within One Week: A Total of 938 Male and Female Smokers 128

Since the city's registration of opium smokers began, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has dispatched inspectors and police officers to actively investigate and suppress unregistered opium smokers in the Chinese area. However, in the Pitu Special District, there are often unlicensed opium smokers entering the area to smoke opium. Tragic Incident of Filicide Occurs in Longhua Town: Shi Aming Appears to Have Mental Illness; After Killing His Son, He Wrapped the Head Carefully; Grieving Grandfather Reported to Police to Arrest Son 129

At about 3 AM the day before yesterday, Liu Songjian, a patrolman at the Longhua Town Branch of West Shanghai, received a report from Shi Asanshi, a native of Haimen. The report stated that he lived in a thatched shed in Pan's Residence, south of Zhahe Temple, making a living by farming. He had two sons, the elder Aming, 38 years old, and the younger Jianming, 34 years old. Aming married a woman named He, and they also had two sons, the elder named Dagou, 12 years old, and the younger named Heimao, just four years old. Aming worked as a worker at the Longzhang Paper Mill in Rihui Bridge outside, leaving early and returning late as usual. However, since last year, he seemed to have symptoms of mental illness, and he hated his younger son Heimao to the bone. Yesterday morning at about 3 AM, Aming took Heimao out in his arms. The father knew something was wrong and immediately followed him. When he reached the Wai Yangqi area behind the Lu's Garden, he suddenly saw that Heimao had been killed, his headless body exposed on the ground, a bloody mess, too horrible to bear. Therefore, he came to report and requested the arrest, etc. Patrolman Liu immediately dispatched Sergeant Tang Chunrong and police officers Wei Duoyi and Zhao Bohang to pursue him. They arrested the murderer Shi Aming at Jijiawan and found a package in his abdomen. Upon inspection, it was a bloody head. Shi Asanshi identified it as the head of his murdered grandson Heimao. They immediately took him back to the station. When questioned, the murderer remained silent, only saying "no way." The patrolman believed that the case involved a human life and ordered the head of the Bao, Wu Quansheng, to report to the District Court for an autopsy. The plaintiff, Shi Asanshi, and the murderer, Shi Aming, father and son, were sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Zhao Genfa, a Rickshaw Owner, Accuses Yin Zhiling of Embezzlement and Fraud; Court Finds Facts Clear, Acquits Yin 130

Yin Zhiling, a member of the Rickshaw Guild, was recently accused by Zhao Genfa, a rickshaw owner from Yancheng, Jiangbei, of embezzlement and fraud, violating Articles 336, Section 2, and 342 of the Criminal Law. In addition to requesting punishment according to the law, he also filed a civil suit. The indictment stated that the plaintiff had ten rickshaws, and all monthly donations, licenses, and custody procedures were entrusted to his cousin Zhao Guanbao. Zhao Guanbao entrusted Yin Zhiling, a member of the Rickshaw Guild, to donate the licenses. There had been no objection for several years. In April of this year, the plaintiff returned to his hometown to manage his farmland and suddenly received a special messenger from Zhao Guanbao to Yancheng, stating that Yin Zhiling had deliberately made things difficult and refused to hand over the rickshaw licenses, so the rickshaws had been suspended for two months. The plaintiff heard this and immediately rushed to Shanghai, asking Chen Zhenzhu to reason with the defendant. However, the defendant claimed that Zhao Guanbao had not cleared his procedures with him and that he had to wait for Zhao to clear them before discussing it. Whether Zhao Guanbao's procedures with the defendant were true or not, it was Zhao Guanbao's personal matter. How could the plaintiff's car licenses be suspended for no reason, resulting in two months of business suspension and huge losses? This clearly violated the criminal law and included a civil suit, requesting a judgment ordering compensation for the two months of lost business, etc. This case was heard by Judge Huang Risheng in the Eighth Criminal Court yesterday morning at 11 AM. The plaintiff, Zhao Genfa, and witness Zhao Guanbao testified about the previous situation. The defendant, Yin Zhiling, also came to court with his defense lawyer Jiang Baoli, stating that Zhao Guanbao had mortgaged his ten rickshaws to Yin for 400 yuan in national currency in August of last year and had written an IOU. This time, because Zhao Guanbao did not hand over the license fees, he could not donate the licenses. However, he did not know that the ownership of the ten rickshaws belonged to the plaintiff beforehand. He submitted the IOU to the court. Witness Bu Zhengang also testified that the loan of 400 yuan was indeed the case, and he and Zhao Guanbao signed it, but he did not know about the mortgage. The court, finding the facts clear, ordered the start of the debate and acquitted Yin Zhiling in court. The plaintiff's civil suit was dismissed.

The small laborers on the fishing boats in the local fish market originally belonged to the North and South Gangs, each occupying the east and west sides of the market pier, respectively. They earned their living by untying mooring lines for the ships, and each shipowner would pay them wages. Recently, the North Gang laborers had fewer ships and their income decreased sharply, so they competed to occupy the South Gang pier. Then, board the Ningxing Steamer in Zhenhai. Arrive in Shanghai on the morning of the 21st.

Firewood Businesses Need Certification from the Guild to Obtain Licenses: The Ministry of Industry Responds to the Chamber of Commerce 140

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Local Miscellaneous Firewood Industry Guild stating that unscrupulous individuals in the city take advantage of the low cost and easy procedures to set up fake businesses. When they see a firewood boat, they do not let it join the guild. Instead, they charge a dry commission of several cents to several yuan, depending on the size of the boat, and allow the firewood merchant to sell freely. Often, after selling 70-80% of the firewood, they rush back to their hometown and sell the remaining 20-30% at a low price to get rid of it. One boat disregards the market situation and dumps the firewood, affecting the price for the boats that arrive later. This situation not only harms the business of guild members but also disrupts the firewood market. The root cause is the people who collect dry commissions. If this is not stopped, the livelihood of the guild members will be in jeopardy. The guild requested that the Ministry of Industry order the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau to strictly ban this practice. In the future, new businesses should be thoroughly reviewed by the guild to ensure they have capital, a business front, and are officially operating. If they are legitimate, the guild will guarantee to the Finance Bureau that they are eligible to receive a business license and open for business. The guild submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry on the [blank] day of last month to allow this to be implemented. Yesterday, they received a notification from the Ministry of Industry, Commerce Division, No. 45527, stating that the Chamber of Commerce's previous request from the Miscellaneous Firewood Industry Guild to allow the guild to apply for business licenses on behalf of its members should be handled by the relevant authorities. When merchants apply for licenses, they should be ordered to provide proof of their situation from the guild. The decision to approve or reject the application should be based on the proof. A document has been sent to the Shanghai Municipal Government for review and response. Now that the response has been received, the Finance Bureau has been instructed to comply. This notification is hereby given.

Ten Programs, Including Siming Nanci, Have Their Broadcast Time Extended: Each Station May Not Exceed Three Hours Per Day, Shanghai Telegraph Responds to the Ningbo Association Yesterday 141

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau previously stipulated that programs such as Siming Nanci, Siming Wenshu, Shanghai Opera, Suzhou Tanci, Small Songs, Qing Songs, Huai Opera, and various school plays, which are related to social interaction, must not exceed two hours of broadcast time. Subsequently, the Siming Nanci broadcaster Sheng Yong-qing and others sent a letter to the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, requesting them to forward it to the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau to request the removal of the restrictions. After deliberation, the bureau decided to generally extend the broadcast time for the above ten programs by one hour. Yesterday, they also replied to the Ningbo Association, stating that in response to the association's letter dated July 11, which forwarded the request from seventeen Siming Nanci broadcasters, including Sheng Yong-qing, to remove the restrictions on Siming Nanci broadcast time, the bureau had previously restricted the broadcast time of ten programs, including Shanghai Opera, because many of the lyrics were related to social education and had been repeatedly requested to be stopped by listeners. Now, the broadcast time for these programs has been extended by one hour to a maximum of three hours per day. Furthermore, they are not allowed to be scheduled between 7:00 PM and 10:00 PM. The previous restrictions have been relaxed. This response is hereby sent to the Ningbo Association for their information. Sincerely, Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, Ministry of Transportation.

The Trial of Zhou Baixing for Beating His Grandfather to Death Concludes: Zhou Meixin Gives Irrelevant Answers, the Defendant's Wife Testifies to What She Knows 143

Zhou Shaoqing, a 63-year-old villager from Zhoujiazhai, Xisanli, Sanlintang, Pudong, had a son, but both the son and daughter-in-law died, each leaving behind a grandson: Zhou Baixing, 19 years old, and Zhou Xuexing. Both grandsons were dissolute and gambled away their money. On April 12 of the lunar calendar, they demanded money from their grandfather Shaoqing, who was frugal and unwilling to support their extravagance. As a result, the two grandsons beat him violently, causing his immediate death. Zhou Baixing fled to his father-in-law, Zhou Xuegen's, house at 139 Luxuezhai, Caojiadu, Shanghai West. Baixing's wife, Zhou Zhou-shi, questioned him about the situation and reported him to the police, who arrested her husband Zhou Baixing and detained him in the District Court. Zhou Xuexing fled and is still at large. After careful investigation, Prosecutor Lei determined that Zhou Baixing should be severely punished in accordance with Article 277, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law for injury resulting in death, and Article 280, Paragraph 1 for injury to a senior relative. Yesterday, Judge Chen Kang-sun presided over the trial. First, the daughter of the deceased, Zhou Meixin (an uneducated simpleton), was interrogated. She stated that she was 21 years old, a local resident, and lived in Zhoujiazhai. Question: Who was Zhou Shaoqing to you, and how did he die? Answer: He was my father. I don't know how he died. I only know that I heard noises in the middle of the night. I got up and saw four people running away, two to the east and two to the south. Question: What did the four people look like? Answer: I didn't see clearly. I only saw my father fall down. Question: What do you call Zhou Baixing? Answer: I call him aunt. But Baixing had been out for three days already. He wasn't home the night before my father died. Question: Why did Baixing usually argue with your father? Answer: They didn't argue. When asked repeatedly about the four murderers who ran east and west, she gave irrelevant answers. Then, Zhou Zhou-shi, 20 years old, from Zhoujiazhai, testified that she lived with her mother in Caojiadu and that her husband was Zhou Baixing. She had a child with him. Because her husband was not engaged in honest work, she lived with her mother. On the morning of April 13, around 7:00 AM, he came. At that time, I was working the night shift, so I was asleep. Question: What did he say? Answer: He didn't say anything. Question: Was he in a state of panic? Answer: He said he came from the countryside. When asked further, he didn't say a word. Question: You testified to the prosecutor that your great-grandfather was beaten badly? Answer: The villagers came to report it. Then, Zhou Baixing testified that Zhou Xuexing beat his grandfather to death. That night, I went to bed early. When I woke up, I heard my grandfather calling for help. I got up and rushed out, but Zhou Xuexing grabbed me and we went out together. Zhou Xuexing and I went east, and three others went west. We took a boat at Zhoujiadu. Question: Why didn't you report it to the police? Answer: I didn't see any patrol officers, and then I didn't see them anymore. Then, Prosecutor Lei gave his opinion, stating that after Zhou Baixing and Zhou Xuexing beat their grandfather to death, they fled to the home of Zhou Baixing's father-in-law in Shanghai. His wife saw that he was in a panic and asked him what happened. He said that his grandfather had been beaten to death. When she asked him again, he didn't say anything. But according to Zhou Meixin's testimony, there were four people. Zhou Baixing's testimony at the Caojiadu police station was the same. But Zhou Baixing saw his grandfather being beaten to death. Shouldn't he have been heartbroken and reported it to the authorities? How could he have run to Shanghai instead? When he arrived at his father-in-law's house, he claimed that his grandfather was acting improperly outside and was beaten to death when he returned. Zhou Meixin testified that someone knocked on the door and called him out. This shows that Zhou Baixing was trying to fabricate a story. Such an unfilial and wicked person should be severely punished. The court appointed the lawyer Sun Ba-wu to defend the defendant. After hearing the legal arguments, the judge adjourned the debate and announced that the verdict would be delivered on the 21st. The defendant was returned to custody.

Kidnapping Bandit Zhang Afu Appeals to the Supreme Court for the Second Time: Now Returned to the High Court Third Branch for Retrial 144

Qian Zhao-fu, a local manager of Yongfeng Timber Company in Nanshi, and Pu Wen-ting, a Wuxi manager of Fuxin Flour Mill, were kidnapped by bandits in the French Concession in the 20s of the Republic, and huge ransoms were demanded. On August 16 of the following year, special agents of the French Concession police solved the case, arresting five bandits including Zheng Shifan, Zhang Afu and Zhang Jiancheng, all locals, and seized firearms and other items. They were sent to the Special Second Court for prosecution. After interrogation, Zheng Shifan and Zhang Afu were each sentenced to life imprisonment, and Zhang Jiancheng was sentenced to 20 years imprisonment. Because he was also involved in another kidnapping case, he was sentenced to death by the Special First Court and executed. Zheng Shifan and Zhang Afu, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed to the Third Branch of the High Court, which later commuted Zheng Shifan's sentence to 12 years imprisonment, and rejected Zhang Afu's appeal. The two criminals were still dissatisfied and appealed to the Supreme Court, which overturned the original verdict and returned the case to the Third Branch of the High Court for retrial. As a result, the Third Branch of the High Court reduced Zheng Shifan's sentence to nine years imprisonment, and still rejected Zhang Afu's appeal. Zheng was still not convinced and filed another appeal to the Supreme Court for retrial. The Supreme Court reviewed the entire case file and found that whether Pu Wen-ting's family had received a ransom negotiation call was unclear, so it overturned the original verdict again and returned the case to the Third Branch of the High Court for retrial. After receiving the case file, the Third Branch of the High Court summoned Zheng Shifan for investigation and interrogation at the First Criminal Court yesterday morning, presided over by Judge Liao. The witnesses Pu Wen-ting and his wife, Pu Huang-shi (represented by Zhu Yu-ting, an employee of Fuxin Mill), and Qin You-yu, an investigator from the French Concession police, were also summoned to court for questioning. Lawyer Fei Xi-zhen from the French Concession Police Department and Zheng's defense lawyer were also present in court. The court questioned the defendant Zheng and the witnesses one by one for over an hour. Zheng continued to deny his involvement in the kidnapping case. The court ordered that the case be further investigated and a date be set for trial. Zheng was returned to custody.

Public Buses in the City Center Should Have Bus Stops: Dong Yu-xiao Submitted a Petition to the Municipal Government Yesterday 145

Huang Yu-zhai, manager of Huizhong Bank on Ningbo Road, submitted a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating, (excerpt): Since the opening of Greater Shanghai, the number of residents in the city center has increased daily, and the population has gradually become prosperous. The China Merchants Public Bus directly reaches the Municipal Government, which is convenient for pedestrians. However, the company's equipment for passengers may be inadequate, especially the bus stop item. The company does not pay attention to this, only planting a parking sign on the side of the road, and not considering the passengers in any other way. The time interval between vehicles is as long as forty minutes. Passengers waiting for the bus suffer from the scorching sun in summer, and the heat is unbearable. There is no shelter from the sun, and the feet are on a road as hot as fire. They not only suffer from the heat, but also from the difficulty of waiting for the bus. Moreover, the weather in summer is unpredictable, with thunder and rain. Once encountered, there is no shelter anywhere. Those with thin clothes on their backs are like chickens falling into the water. It is inevitable for the old to stumble and the young to fall, and they may suffer from heatstroke or illness, endangering their lives. The harm is even greater. In winter, the north wind is whistling and rain and snow are flying. The cold penetrates through heavy clothes. Standing and waiting for a long time is unbearable on the icy road. Or, snow accumulates above the ankles, making walking difficult. This is really inconvenient for passengers. Although the concessions do not have this equipment either, why should we be fussy about the Chinese areas? Because the situation in the Chinese areas is different and cannot be compared with the concessions. The concessions have prosperous markets and shops are densely packed. One can avoid the wind and sun at any time and anywhere. The city center area is not like this. There are open fields all around, and there is no way to avoid it. This situation is not only what I have witnessed, but also what I have experienced. Therefore, it is urgent to establish public wind and rain bus stops in the city center to benefit pedestrians and facilitate their transportation. Since the opening of Greater Shanghai, the construction can be said to be perfect, but the matter of bus stops has not yet been considered. Therefore, I take the liberty to petition Your Honor on behalf of the citizens of the city center to order the China Merchants Public Bus Company to establish these bus stops as soon as possible. This matter concerns road administration and benefits pedestrians. It can certainly be accomplished soon. I beg Your Honor to consider the human situation and order it to be implemented, which would be a great virtue. (Excerpt)

The Jiangwan Road Massacre: Two Men and Women Dead, One Woman Injured, The Murderer Yang Chunyi Fled Without a Trace 146

Zhang Longhai, a 41-year-old man from Pudong, living at 131 Binxi Road, Jiangwan Road, married Shen Cui'e (29 years old), a woman from Jiangwan. At around 9:00 PM last night, Zhang was enjoying the cool air in the living room after dinner. His wife Shen and sister-in-law Shen Zhifang (18 years old) were sitting beside him, chatting and laughing, creating a very happy scene. Suddenly, Yang Chunyi arrived, carrying a package of clothes, and broke into the room. Because they knew each other, they did not suspect anything. Yang opened the package and pulled out a pistol from his trousers pocket. He rushed into the living room and fired several shots in succession. Zhang Longhai was shot twice in the abdomen and died from his injuries. Zhang's wife, Shen, and sister-in-law, Zhifang, were terrified at the sight and tried to escape to the wasteland behind the house. Unexpectedly, Yang also chased after them, firing wildly. The bullets were like strings of beads. One bullet hit Shen Cui'e in the heart, and she fell to the ground and died on the spot. Zhifang was also shot once near her right breast. The bullet pierced her back, and she was gasping for breath, with blood gushing out. The murderer, seeing that his purpose had been achieved, quickly ran away. The maid heard the alarm and gathered the neighbors, and reported the incident to the Jiangwan Police Station, which sent police to the scene. But the murderer had already fled far away. The police were only able to take the items left behind by the murderer back to the station for filing. The seriously injured Shen Zhifang was quickly hired a car to Baolong Hospital for treatment. It is said that the injuries were severe and her life was in danger. The two male and female bodies have been reported to the local court for inspection by the Public Security Bureau. (The two bodies were photographed by Jingyi Photography Studio)

Letter to the Editor 151

Dear Editor, We have received a letter from Mr. Zhan Wei-hui, stating that he recently read an article in the Shanghai News column of the Shen Bao about a child falling into the river at the Minhang ferry. Some of the details are inconsistent with the facts. The ferry does not allow idlers to stay and enjoy the cool air, and we have repeatedly advised and posted notices. However, recently, due to the major renovation of the pier, some residents are taking advantage of the fact that the iron gate cannot be locked and have reverted to their old habits. At about 9:00 PM on the 11th of this month, a large number of residents were lying on the ferry. The manager persuaded them to leave, but to no avail. The undersigned personally went to wake them up one by one. At this time, there was a sound of something falling into the water from the east side. It was impossible to investigate in the darkness. In the deep of night, two ruffians came, claiming that their son had drowned, saying that the undersigned had injured him by falling into the water and had assaulted him, beating him on the abdomen, back, and arms, and stealing a five-section flashlight. The above facts were witnessed by others. Now, fearing that the outside world may misunderstand the truth and be confused by the rumors, we have specially entrusted our lawyer to send a letter to your newspaper, requesting a correction. Therefore, we will send this letter on your behalf and hope that you will publish it in the corrections column to clarify the truth. To the Shen Bao, Lawyer Zai Bao-ji.

Sports News

My Country's Football Team's European Tour 152

— Written and sent by Captain Li Huitang

Rangoon, Eighth Day (Continued)

(June 28th) The first match had 23,000 spectators, breaking the local record for attendance. Yesterday's match had even more, reportedly over 28,000. Fans also filled the treetops and rooftops outside the stadium, but these numbers were not included in the official count. The strong appeal of our team is evident. Today is Sunday. Thanks to the kindness of the overseas Chinese community, a small steamboat was chartered for a day's outing. The boat included a Burmese dance troupe and music for entertainment. Over two hundred overseas Chinese of both genders participated. Along the way, there were occasional showers and sunshine, laughter and conversation. The scenery of the rivers and mountains was captivating. Each time we reached a small port, we disembarked to tour the market, where residents, whether Burmese or Chinese, rushed to tell each other that the Chinese football team had arrived. As the sun began to set, we returned by the same route. By the time we arrived back at our residence, the city was illuminated. At 7 PM, we attended a tea party hosted by the Chinese Buddhist Research Association and a banquet hosted by the Minyou Club in succession. We have only been here for a few days, but we have been overwhelmed with invitations. Some people even wanted to entertain our team but couldn't due to our tight schedule. The warmth of the overseas Chinese community is truly touching.

(June 29th) The final match is scheduled for 5 PM today. We haven't eliminated our formidable opponents yet, and none of us dare to rest easy. The football authorities, recognizing the previous day's overflowing crowd and chaotic conditions, were determined not to repeat the mistake. They took early precautions, deploying an additional five hundred police officers and cavalry to maintain order inside and outside the stadium. Tickets were sold early at each gate, and the doors were closed as soon as they were sold out. It is said that three to four thousand people were unable to enter that day. The crowd inside was definitely more than a thousand larger than the second match. The opponent today is a team of All-Burma players, combining the best of the best. The Chinese were confident in our team's complete victory, while the Burmese were determined to avenge their previous defeat with this gathering of heroes. The Burmese governor issued an order to close all government offices early to allow officials to attend. The governor himself will also be present. The importance of this match is clear. At 5:05 PM, the following players were ready for battle. The score was 2-0 at halftime, and the final score was 4-0. Li Huitang scored two goals, while Yang Shuiyi and Tan Jiangbo each scored one.

Bao Jiaping

Li Tiansheng, Mai Shaohan

Chen Zhenhe, Liang Rongzhao, Zhang Xianyuan

Zheng Jimin, Tan Jiangbo, Li Huitang, Sun Jinshun, Yang Shuiyi

Before the match, the two teams stood respectfully at the foot of the platform. The captains introduced their teammates and shook hands with the Burmese governor before the game began. The Burmese team continued to attack using their short-passing skills. Fortunately, our defense performed brilliantly, preventing them from scoring. It was drizzling that day, and the field was wet and the ball slippery, making it difficult to control. However, the heavy ball favored shooting, giving our team a slight advantage. For the first fifteen minutes, although we launched numerous attacks, we couldn't break through. However, our tactics were effective, giving us the upper hand. The spectators expected our team to win. In the 25th minute, we were awarded a free kick 25 yards from the goal. Li Huitang fired a low shot into the net. The goalkeeper's view was blocked, so he couldn't save it. With the gate breached, our offense became even more fierce. Yang Jiangbo's header added another goal. The first half ended with a score of 2-0. Switching sides, the opposing team lacked stamina and struggled to defend. Fortunately, their goalkeeper made miraculous saves, stopping many shots. Yang Shuiyi, short in stature but full of ideas, attacked on the right, tricked the left defender, and scored with a diagonal shot, making it 3-0. At this point, the outcome of the match was decided. Although the opponents continued to struggle, our defense was solid, and they were not allowed to cross the line. In the 52nd minute, Li Huitang received a pass from Xiao Heitan, dribbled past two defenders, and scored with a left-footed shot, making it 4-0. Our team won decisively. The overseas Chinese celebrated joyfully. Some were so excited that they lifted me onto their shoulders and carried me from the field to the dressing room. This was due to their extreme happiness and their genuine love for our team, which cannot be described in words. The opposing team had evenly matched players, each with excellent skills, but their coordination was poor and they lacked shooting ability. As the saying goes, "For every foot of height, there's ten feet of magic," so there was nothing they could do. Our team's performance that day was perfect. Zhang Xianyuan contributed the most in this match since joining the team. He was overjoyed after the game. Zhang Xianyuan is a center back. I am now even more convinced of this. Jiang Bo has been playing forward in all three matches. It is a pity that his talents as a defender have not been revealed. However, our team has had too many forward injuries lately, so he was moved to the front line to provide immediate help. There was no better option. He has been instrumental in our attacks in every match, allowing me to penetrate deeper and contribute significantly. Together with my flexible copper head, we dominated the area and achieved numerous feats. Sun Jinshun, despite being overweight, has been working hard in every match lately, a stark contrast to the first half of the tour. Others like Jia Ping, Tiansheng, Rongzhao, and Zhenhe have also been praised by Chinese and foreign spectators alike. Since I joined the football world, I have always had good plans whenever I arrive in a new place. Perhaps this is due to good luck, as I have had this good fortune for over a decade. This time in Burma, I have been able to attract special attention in all three matches. As a result, the number nine shirt has become the focus of attention for spectators and opposing defenders. At my age, to have such good results is truly gratifying for fans. After the match, I saw that Burma's football level is not inferior to that of other places in Southeast Asia. As for individual teams, the Burmese police team is capable of competing with any team in East Asia. Their excellent dribbling, skillful short passing, agility, and clever positioning are all things we can learn from. It is a pity that their shooting is slow, they lack stamina, and their heading is sluggish. Otherwise, even though our team is strong, we would probably have to bow down and acknowledge their superiority. In the evening, as our team was leaving the next morning, the overseas Chinese community held a farewell banquet. Nearly three hundred prominent Chinese and Western figures gathered together. The scale of the event was unmatched by any sports banquet in China. Consul Cai presided over the event. The local police chief (also vice president of the football association) gave a speech, starting by saying, "Originally, I was going to order you to be deported long ago because you have caused a sensation in the city, disturbing the peace, and disrupting the city's traffic order since you arrived." His humorous and unexpected remarks caused laughter throughout the hall, showing how much the Burmese value our team. Then, Director Rong and Huitang gave speeches, expressing deep gratitude for the care and affection shown by people from all walks of life. Finally, each member of the team was presented with a commemorative medal, and I received a special award of a silver bowl. After three cheers, the event ended. As it was not yet late, we were invited to a dance hall to relax. The overseas Chinese invited us to drink, promising that no one would leave sober. By the time we returned to our residence, the clock struck three. We were exhausted, so we fell asleep without packing.

(June 30th) The eight days of our stay in Rangoon have come to an end in the blink of an eye. Looking back, we are filled with gratitude for the warm care and protection we received from the overseas Chinese community in all aspects of our matches and accommodations. Today, as we say farewell, we feel a sense of sadness. At 8:30 AM, hundreds of members of the overseas Chinese community came to see us off. They rode in many cars, led by a band. We paraded through the streets, with firecrackers exploding along the way. The roadsides were packed with people eager to catch a final glimpse of our team. The scene was even grander and more enthusiastic than when we arrived. At 9:30 AM, we boarded the ship. At 10 AM, we set sail westwards, waving goodbye as we headed towards Calcutta, India.

Note: During the farewell reception, we invited Burma to join the Far Eastern Games as a member and send a team to Shanghai in 1938 to participate in the competition. If this becomes a reality, the football competition at the Far Eastern Games will become even more exciting, and our country will have another strong opponent.

Swimming Competition Against Guangdong Suffers Setback, Xiqing Wins by a Narrow Margin of 23 to 21 154

Education News

Zhejiang Schools Youth Training, Education Department Uniforms Youth League Headquarters Organization, Stipulates Provisional Regulations for General League Headquarters Organization 165

(Central News Agency) Hangzhou, 15th Dispatch. In order to implement youth training and enhance education effectiveness, the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education has stipulated and promulgated the Zhejiang Provincial Youth League Outline, ordering all levels of schools to comply and implement it. Details have been repeatedly reported in the press. It is now learned that all public and private schools that have implemented this training will establish formal league headquarters after the autumn semester begins. In order to standardize the organization of each league headquarters, the Education Department has specifically stipulated the Provisional Regulations for Youth League Headquarters and issued them to all schools for compliance. According to sources from the General League Headquarters, each league headquarters will have a general affairs, organization, and training section, each with a director and several staff members to handle section affairs. Except for the necessary full-time personnel, all positions will be held concurrently by existing personnel from various agencies and will not be paid separately. The responsibilities of each section are as follows: (A) The duties of the General Affairs Section are: 1. To manage the custody of the team's seals; 2. To manage the drafting, writing, and proofreading of all documents and the preservation of files; 3. To manage the editing and printing of various publications of the Youth League; 4. To manage the compilation and printing of various statistical reports of the Youth League; 5. To manage all accounting, general affairs, and affairs not belonging to other sections; (B) The duties of the Organization Section are: 1. To draft various regulations and forms for the team's organization; 2. To handle registration matters within the team's organization; 3. To guide and promote the organization of the Youth League; 4. To manage certificates, badges, and flags; 5. To investigate all organizational activities within the team; 6. To compile various reports on the team's organization; 7. To handle other matters related to the team's organization; (C) The duties of the Training Section are: 1. To draft various regulations, charts, and tables for the team's training; 2. To guide all training activities within the team; 3. To plan technical training matters; 4. To handle matters related to education; 5. To handle all assessment and inspection matters; 6. To compile various reports on the team's training; 7. To handle other matters related to the team's training. It is also heard that the league headquarters may establish a design committee and other special committees upon approval by the General League President. The organization of these committees will be determined separately and submitted for approval.

Seven Academic Organizations Actively Preparing for Joint Annual Meeting, Announcing Member Guidelines and Annual Meeting Schedule, Approved by Transportation Authorities for Member Discounts 166

The seven organizations of the Chinese Science Society, the Chinese Mathematical Society, the Chinese Physical Society, the Chinese Geographical Society, the Chinese Chemical Society, the Chinese Botanical Society, and the Chinese Zoological Society will hold their joint annual meeting in Beiping from the 18th to the 20th of next month. The following are excerpts from the member guidelines and annual meeting schedule:

Member Guidelines

(1) This year's joint annual meeting is scheduled to be held in Beiping from August 16th to 20th. Group tours will be arranged after the closing ceremony. (2) Members of the Chinese Mathematical Society, the Chinese Physical Society, and the Chinese Chemical Society, as well as members of the Physical Science and Engineering Science groups of the Chinese Science Society, will be accommodated at Yenching University. Members of the Zoological Society, the Botanical Society, and the Geographical Society, as well as members of the Biological Science and Social Science groups of the Chinese Science Society, will be accommodated at Tsinghua University. (3) Each member is allowed to bring one family member. Guests, except those specially invited by the joint annual meeting, will not be entertained. (4) Upon registration at the meeting, each member shall receive a joint annual meeting badge upon presentation of the annual meeting fee receipt. All gatherings, meals, accommodations, transportation, and banquets during the annual meeting will be provided upon presentation of the badge. (5) To facilitate arrangements, the deadline for registration for the meeting is temporarily set as August 5th. (6) The general office of the annual meeting organizing committee is located at No. 22 Nanchang Street, Beiping, inside the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture. (7) After the closing of the annual meeting, members may organize tours according to their personal interests, at their own expense.

Annual Meeting Schedule

The schedule of the joint annual meeting has been finalized and is announced as follows: August 16th, registration in the afternoon at Yenching University and Tsinghua University, Beiping. August 17th, registration in the morning at the same locations. Opening ceremony at 10:00 AM at Tsinghua University. Luncheon hosted by Tsinghua University. 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, business meeting of the Chinese Science Society at Tsinghua University. 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM, lectures by Su Buqing and Bing Zhi. 5:00 PM, tour of the academic exhibition at Tsinghua University. August 18th, 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, presentation of papers by each academic society and groups of similar nature of the Chinese Science Society: Mathematics, Physics, and Chemistry at Yenching University; Zoology, Botany, and Geography at Tsinghua University. Luncheon hosted by Yenching University. 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, business meeting of the Chinese Science Society at Yenching University. 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM, public lectures. 5:00 PM, tour of the academic exhibition at Yenching University. August 19th, 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, presentation of papers at Peking University. 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM, public lectures, including Weng Wenhao. Luncheon hosted jointly by the Beiping Research Institute, Beiping Library, Palace Museum, Peking University, Normal University, Pingmin University, Sino-French University, Jing Sheng Biological Research Institute, and the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture. 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, group tours of Beiping cultural institutions. 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM, experimental demonstrations by the Chinese Physiological Society at Peking Union Medical College. 6:00 PM, banquet hosted by the Beiping Municipal Government. August 20th, morning, presentation of papers by each academic society: Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, Zoology, Botany, and Geography; business meetings of each academic society. Luncheon, picnic at the Summer Palace. 6:00 PM, banquet for all members. 7:00 PM, social gathering. 10:00 PM, closing ceremony at Yenching University.

Group Excursions

After the annual meeting, members will participate in group excursions, including: Group A: Mentougou, Tanzhe Temple, Jietai Temple, Zhoukoudian, etc. Group B: Mentougou, Tanzhe Temple, Jietai Temple, etc. Group C: Nankou, Qinglongqiao, Ming Tombs, etc. Group D: Zhangjiakou, Datong, Yungang Grottoes, etc. Group E: Western Hills and surrounding areas of Beiping. The cost of the excursion is 20 to 15 yuan per person per group.

Travel Discounts

For this annual meeting, members traveling on national railways have been granted special permission by the Ministry of Railways to receive a 25% discount on one-way tickets and a 50% discount on round-trip tickets. This applies to all express trains. The effective period is from August 1st to August 31st, to show preferential treatment. If members travel by waterway, discounts may also be obtained when taking national-operated China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Minsheng Industrial Company ships. The China Travel Service has been specially entrusted to handle ticket changes and accommodations for members traveling to various locations.

Education Subsidies for Mongolia, Tibet, and Muslims Have Been Allocated, Totaling 522,000 Yuan 167

The central government, through the central education authorities, has allocated 522,000 yuan from the national treasury for the 25th fiscal year as subsidies for promoting education related to Mongolia, Tibet, and Muslims in relevant provinces. It is reported that the amount of funds allocated to the subsidized provinces has been decided by the central education authorities in a meeting, and the education authorities will soon issue notices to the provinces and cities concerned. The subsidized provinces include Guizhou, Yunnan, Gansu, Xikang, Qinghai, Ningxia, Suiyuan, Xinjiang, Chahar, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Hunan, and Tibet, totaling thirteen provinces. The amount of subsidies ranges from 18,000 yuan to tens of thousands or even thousands of yuan, depending on the actual needs of the respective projects. Most of the funds will be used to establish normal schools and primary schools for Mongolia, Tibet, and Muslims, including 20,000 yuan for the expenses of the Mongolian Cultural Center, and for compiling and printing textbooks for Mongolia, Tibet, and Muslim education, as well as subsidies for students from Mongolia, Tibet, and Muslim regions to enter domestic vocational schools, totaling 522,000 yuan. The detailed allocation will be communicated to the subsidized provinces and departments by the Ministry of Education via telegram in the near future.

Soochow Law School Adds Commercial Law Department 177

The Soochow University Law School in this city has always been known for its excellent management and outstanding academic performance. Recently, it was heard that the school, to meet the needs of the times, facilitate people from all walks of life, supplement their knowledge of commercial law, and enhance their work efficiency, has specially added a Commercial Law Department starting this semester. The curriculum is divided into required and elective courses. Elective students may select courses related to their interests or occupations from the courses offered by the school and receive a certificate of completion for each course passed. Business News

Finance: Last Day of August Futures, Margin Money Continues to Decline, Swap Still Requires Over Three Yuan, Resulting in Further Drop of Ninety Cents 181

Yesterday was the last day of trading for the August gold futures market. Although the settlement price was only two yuan apart, the swap still required more than three yuan. The longs continued to close positions, resulting in a further drop. It was noted that at the beginning of the morning, the overseas silver market saw London silver trading flat with New York, and market sources said that after the market closed, there were Indian buyers on the board, but no sellers, so the forward silver price did not move. Exchange rates saw only minor fluctuations. London gold rose by one and a half pence. The Central Bank's posted exchange rates showed London and New York flat, and the Customs gold unit rose by two li. The standard margin money price was posted at 1129 yuan, and pre-market trading opened at 32 yuan zero. Dingkang, Hengchang, and Yong Lue sold and fell. The morning opening was slightly higher, but then it was flat and weak. However, because the swap pre-trade retreated from three and a half yuan to within three yuan, it rose slightly once. The HSBC bank's posted exchange rates showed London and New York flat, and major players slightly cut long positions, but still fell. The silver equalization tax was announced to decrease by two five. At this time, there was still much fluctuation. After the market opened, the longs continued to close positions. Because the settlement price was only 29 yuan, and the swap still required more than three yuan, it was revealed that the market lacked support, resulting in the weakest point at noon. The swap was posted by the longs at three to three and a half yuan. The half-day market situation is recorded below:

The morning opening was at 113.1 yuan eight jiao, slightly higher by one jiao compared to the previous closing. Futai, Yong Hengchang Yong sold from one yuan nine jiao to one yuan six jiao, and the swap price pre-trade decreased from three and a half yuan to within three yuan. Tongtaichang Futai Yong bought in, rising to two yuan three jiao. Yuanchang, Yong Da Decheng, Yuan Fa Yong Heng sold, and although the HSBC posted exchange rates were flat, the price still retreated to one yuan six jiao. Fuxing Yong Da Decheng still accepted, rising to two yuan. Da Decheng and Yuan Fa Yong took profits at the high. The silver equalization tax was announced to decrease by two five. At this time, the situation fluctuated. After the market opened, Fuxing Yong Dingkang Yuancheng Yong Da came in to sell, and the price retreated to zero seven jiao. Daheng once rose to one yuan two jiao, but because the settlement price was less than two yuan apart, but the swap still required three yuan three jiao, the longs closed positions. Jiuda floated long and sold the strip, and the price fell again to zero seven jiao. The afternoon closing was at 1130 yuan eight jiao.

The settlement price, according to the Central Bank's standard margin money price, was posted at 1129 yuan, only increasing by less than two yuan according to the closing price, less than the two yuan increase compared to the previous closing. The registration price for this month is 1127 yuan, August is 1131 yuan, and September is 114 yuan. The morning top-up price was 1127 yuan, and the red gold price was 1139 yuan eight jiao. The spot market situation was stable. Tianjin goods were sold by Shengyuan Yong to Yongfeng for 140 taels, adding 16 yuan. The purchase price for cooked red was 13 yuan higher, and the selling price was 16 and a half yuan, but there were no buyers.

There were not many transactions in the market. In summary, Yicheng, Fuxing Yong, Da Heng, Da Decheng, Yuancheng Yong, Tong Taichang, Futai Yong, Qingfa Yong, etc., were on the buying side, and Huixiang, Daf Fa Yong, Jiu Da Hengchang Yong, Da Feng Heng, Dingkang, etc., were on the selling side. Yuancheng Yong and Fuxing Yong went in first and then out, and Futai Yong and Tian Decheng went out first and then in.

It was observed that the half-day market situation was still weak. The morning opening was at 11312 yuan eight jiao, and the afternoon closing was at 1130 yuan eight jiao. The highest price was 1132 yuan three jiao, and the lowest price was 1130 yuan seven jiao, with a range of one yuan six jiao. The pre-market trading for the August-September futures market was posted by the longs at three to three and a half yuan. Wanxing once posted it at around three and a half yuan. Da Decheng, Ruixing, Yuancheng Yong, Jingfu Yicheng, and Da Feng Heng Fu Yu Tong Feng Heng immediately bought in, retreating to within three yuan. The afternoon closing was at yuan three jiao, and after the closing, it was three yuan two three jiao.

After the Gold Exchange issued a notice increasing the handling fee, the brokers of the exchange held a meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss it. They decided to sympathize with the exchange, but requested that the implementation be postponed until Monday of next week. The original single-sided commission of jiao, excluding the broker's incentive bonus of 25%, meant that the exchange received 7.5 fen of national currency per strip on one side. This was reduced to 7.5 fen net for both entering and exiting, totaling one jiao. In other words, the net handling fee that brokers should pay to the exchange is 3.75 li per strip on one side. The chairman of the association negotiated with the exchange, and then a decision was made.

Securities: Government Bond Trading Mostly Swaps, Market Prices Mixed, 96 Now Inverted 183

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange saw the market situation dominated by swap transactions, resulting in a fluctuating trend. However, there was some selling from the financial sector, and confidence gradually weakened. Furthermore, the Guangdong authorities' forceful seizure of the Bank of China's customs tax deposits further caused the longs to start shaking. Militarily, it seemed that contact had already been made. The result of the Second Plenary Session of the Central Committee was likely to first seek domestic unification, and then resist foreign aggression. This meant that the southwest was a prerequisite problem, and the restoration of public bonds' discount for cash also meant that the financial sector would inevitably see an outflow of spot goods. The future was difficult to be optimistic about. The market initially opened with number 37 buying in and remained stable, but later numbers 4, 11, and 14 sold Class C bonds, gradually weakening and turning slightly negative by one or two jiao. Selling pressure remained strong at the close, but Class E bonds did not see a fall, only slightly negative by one jiao. The rest continued to be slightly negative by two or three jiao. The forward price of Class A bonds returned to the previous one jiao. The overall trend for the day was that Class E bonds were the most firm, rising by a good three jiao. Class D bonds also rose by a good three jiao five fen due to number 37's buyback. The rest consistently continued to be slightly negative by five fen, one jiao, to two and a half jiao. The 96 forward price was slightly negative by three jiao, and the recent price was slightly negative by five fen, resulting in an inverted market. The total number of transactions was 4.26 million yuan. The results of the price increases and decreases are listed in the table on the left (unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan).

Hardware 184

American Black Iron Factory is Doing Very Well 185

Yesterday, the hardware market was quiet. Ninety pounds of British tinplate, 150 boxes handled by the Henan group, were sold for $18.60. White lead sheets, sizes 5 and 6, were bought in large quantities by battery factories; the price for No. 5 was $128, and for No. 6 was $126. American black iron sheets had a very good trend in the market yesterday. Enamel factories, toy factories, and machine factories all made purchases, so the market was quite strong, opening at $11.75 per dan. British steel plates, I-beams, water pipes, flower garden lead wire, and shear mouth iron were all ordered by various groups and local factories, but the quantity was small, so the price did not fluctuate.
