Telegraphic Special Edition

After Installing a Telephone 214

— Jì Guān

Points to Note for Users

The benefits of telephones are well known to ordinary people. Once installed, they can be connected at any time. Whether near or far, both parties can talk as if they were face to face. The United States is the most developed country in terms of telephones. Its people regard the use of telephones as a necessity in daily life. Although my country's progress is slow, in recent years, the development of the telephone industry has also been increasing day by day, which shows a glimpse of the society's willingness to use it.

After the telephone is installed, making calls is naturally not a problem, but users should also understand that to maintain calls and make quick calls with this telephone, they should usually pay attention to it. Although this is common knowledge, it seems worth discussing.

(A) When installing a telephone, a deposit must be paid. This deposit is equivalent to the price of the machine. If it is not used and removed in the future, the telephone company will naturally have to return the full amount. However, users must know that the telephone is the property of the telephone company. During the period of use, it is also the property of the user. Usually, they should pay attention to protecting the machine parts to avoid losses and compensation.

(B) Whether the telephone is installed indoors on a desk or hung high on the wall, the new machine is beautiful in style and can be used as a decoration even if it is a tool. However, after being used for a long time, it gradually becomes dirty and damaged, and even the machine cord is knotted and the magnetic paint is peeling off. It is the user's fault to let it go naturally without cherishing it. Therefore, users should clean and wipe their telephones at any time (with a dry cloth or broom) so that they can last for a long time without breaking.

(C) Dampness and moisture are most easily absorbed into the telephone cord, affecting the call. Therefore, wet cloths, towels, and damp objects must not be placed on the telephone at will to avoid affecting the use.

(D) If you need to personally call someone to talk after receiving a call, you cannot hang up the receiver at this time. If it is a desk phone, it can be placed on the desk without any problem. If it is a wall phone, there is no way to hang it up in a hurry. Often, the receiver is allowed to drop and hang directly next to the machine. If this is done repeatedly, the telephone cord is very easily damaged. If a hook or hanger is pre-installed, this problem can be avoided. (The edge of the cover plate of the magneto telephone can be used to temporarily hang the receiver, but it is also quite easy to slip off.)

(E) The telephone number of this machine, if it is an automatic telephone, is clearly marked on the central round piece on the dial. It is clear at a glance. However, the magneto or common battery telephone lacks it. It is best for the user to write it himself and stick it on the machine so that when making a call or if someone asks about the number of this machine, or if they want him to call back, they can temporarily forget it without having to look it up.

(F) Users who often need to make calls should make a list of their telephone numbers and hang it next to the machine so that they can get it at a glance. The telephone numbers of the fire brigade and the police station in charge should also be included in it to prevent problems before they occur and to feel more convenient in an emergency.

(G) If the telephone is not working, the telephone company will send a worker to repair it, or if the rental fee is due, the telephone company will send a staff member to collect it. Those who enter and leave the user's house wear symbols or badges. If there is any doubt, they can be proven. To prevent the mingling of petty thieves, users should also pay sufficient attention to this point.

(H) Users who use magneto or common battery telephones may think that the operators are not serving well (such as being rude and scolding, etc.) or that the connection is delayed. If it is true, you do not have to argue with each other on the machine and have a quarrel. You should report the real situation and the date and time of the call to the telephone company. The telephone company can check it out immediately and punish the operators according to the rules.

When installing a telephone, the telephone company will do its best to provide common convenience for making calls. On the user's side, it is nothing more than hoping that the telephone can always be kept in good condition without having to be repaired from time to time. However, since the telephone is installed in someone's home, this part of the machine is entirely up to the user to maintain and cherish it. Using it well can also increase the speed of calls and reduce unnecessary troubles. This is actually beneficial to both parties. I hope that those who install the machine will pay attention to it.

Giving Gifts by Telegram 215

— Yǒulǐ

Giving gifts by telegram, the telegram arrives, and the gift certificate also arrives. The delivery boy is polite, and also serves as a gift messenger. However, according to the usual custom, the messenger's tip ranges from a few cents to several yuan depending on the thickness of the gift. The delivery boy who acts as a gift messenger must absolutely not ask for or accept it.

In the past, social telegrams could only send congratulatory or condolence messages. The recipient of such a telegram knew that relatives and friends in the distance were expressing deep sympathy for their weddings, funerals, or celebrations. In terms of etiquette, it was only to express their heart. However, in social customs, internal expression is certainly important, but the gift of material things cannot be avoided. Since there is gift-giving by telegram, the heart and the gift actually arrive, and the recipient receives considerable comfort in both spirit and matter. Increasing the friendship between the two parties, this method is really thoughtful.

Speaking of giving gifts, I personally feel that it is a troublesome thing, especially when sending them to a distance? After opening a draft through the post office or bank, you still need to write a letter yourself for congratulations or condolences and send the draft together by registered mail. This letter for giving gifts, whether it should use "a hundred years of harmony" or "condolences on your loss," I, who am frugal, often feel that it is "quite troublesome." Now, you only need to hand the gift money to the telegraph office and send a simple telegram. The telegraph office also has ready-made words for the telegram, which you can choose and use at your discretion. The cost of the telegram is limited, and the trouble saved is a lot. I dare to say that everyone feels convenient.

People who are handling weddings, funerals, and celebrations! Don't think that your relatives or friends are far away and may not have time to give gifts or have forgotten to give gifts. You must know that giving gifts by telegram is especially fast. It can be delivered as scheduled on the day it is sent. Wait until the delivery boy enters the door to believe that your relatives and friends are generous and affectionate, not only have they not lost etiquette, but the gift they have given is a gift certificate that is formal and can be cashed immediately! Etiquette is about reciprocity, and you can certainly praise it as "the best in social interaction."

Various Improvements Regarding Radio Broadcasting Stations 216

In recent years, radio broadcasting in our country has gradually aroused the interest of the general public, and the installation of radios has also been increasing day by day. It is reported that the Ministry of Communications issued 42,565 radio licenses by the end of last year, and 53,634 licenses by mid-June of this year, an increase of 11,069 over the end of last year. If this number is compared with Japan and the United States, it is certainly far behind, but it is also a very good phenomenon in my country's initial stage. Moreover, in fact, this number is definitely less than the actual number, because there are many cases where those who install machines have not registered, and this is probably an inevitable stage.

The Ministry of Communications recently felt that the power of the Shanghai and Beiping broadcasting stations run by the ministry was very small, which was not enough to give full play to their effectiveness. It is now reported that it has been decided to change the original 200-watt station in Shanghai to 2,000 watts, and the original 200-watt station in Beiping to 1,000 watts. All renovation plans have been ordered to be decided by the respective stations and submitted to the Ministry for review. It is expected that this renovation will be implemented soon. It is also reported that it will actively improve the broadcasting program, especially the educational program, and strive to enrich it, such as hiring celebrities to give lectures and teaching various sciences to increase the common sense of general listeners.

The World Games are scheduled to be held in Berlin, Germany on August 1. The athletes participating in our country are all outstanding figures. In order to promote sports, the Ministry of Communications has decided to receive the above sports news from the International Radio Station's Liuhang Receiving Station, and then connect it to the Central Broadcasting Station via long-distance telephone lines for national broadcasting.

The Ministry of Communications reported that the Jiuda Broadcasting Station in Suzhou increased its power privately, and even broadcast Cantonese music during the period of suspension of entertainment due to the death of Chairman Hu Zhan, and has sent personnel to investigate and confirm it. It has been punished by suspending broadcasting for two weeks as a warning.

Measures of the Ministry of Communications to Maintain Long-Distance Telephone Lines 217

In order to increase the efficiency of repairing telecommunication line obstacles, the Ministry of Communications stipulated the method of repairing telecommunication line obstacles in September last year. All lines under the jurisdiction of various bureaus and offices should be paid attention to by engineers, business directors, testers, branch chiefs, or business personnel at any time. If obvious anomalies occur, the internal and external lines should be inspected separately. If it is found that the obstacle occurs outside the bureau, a work order should be issued immediately to order the workers to rush to investigate and repair it as soon as possible without any delay. As for the time for line workers to repair line obstacles, except for very serious disasters that cannot be repaired due to insufficient manpower, the time of blocking the money, day or night, must not exceed the following regulations: (1) Important lines, 24 hours: (2) Secondary and ordinary lines, 30 hours. Since then, the rate of repairing money obstacles has increased a lot.

Since the beginning of this spring, long-distance telephone line projects in various provinces have been gradually completed and opened for business, which is very important for communication in all aspects. It is urgently necessary to maintain it conscientiously. If the lines occasionally lose their balance, there will be problems such as induced noise. It is difficult to hear clearly when talking. Therefore, the method of repairing the electric money line should be paid attention to carefully and should not be slackened.

In addition, the cross positions and methods of each telephone line have been properly configured, and no changes are allowed. Drawings should be drawn immediately to instruct the workers in charge of the section to be familiar with the number of pairs of telephone lines under their jurisdiction and the cross position method to avoid errors. When the Qian workers test the money, they must conduct it on a money testing pole equipped with a money testing clip. After the test is completed, the money testing clip must be wiped clean, connected properly, and tightened. Do not cut off the lines arbitrarily. Furthermore, the Ministry of Communications has long stipulated the entrance of each long-distance telephone line into the bureau and office. The other intermediate bureaus must not arbitrarily cut off the line to introduce it, or connect other single money to prevent hindering the call.

The above measures have been ordered to be followed by the various electrical administration bureaus.

Ministry of Communications Actively Organizes Ship Radio Stations 218

It has been observed that many of the ship radio stations installed on Chinese merchant ships are poorly equipped and maintained, resulting in low communication efficiency, which greatly affects navigation safety. It is heard that the Ministry of Communications, in order to improve the communication efficiency of various ship radio stations, has stipulated the following organizational measures:

(1) When Chinese merchant ships equipped with ship radio stations arrive in Shanghai, the captain or their agent shall immediately submit a written report to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, which shall notify the Shanghai International Radio Station to dispatch engineers or technicians for inspection.

(2) When technicians from the International Radio Station inspect ship radio stations, they should pay attention to the following points: 1. Whether the transmitting and receiving equipment is well maintained; 2. Whether the power supply equipment is appropriate; 3. Whether the frequency of the transmitter is accurate; 4. Whether the antenna method, height, and length are appropriate; 5. Whether there are spare transmitters and receivers and automatic alarm machines; 6. Whether the batteries are well maintained; 7. Whether the location and equipment of the radio room are appropriate; 8. Whether the radio station and radio operators have licenses; whether the radio operators' skills are excellent; how many radio operators are there in total; 9. Whether the wireless compass is accurate; 10. Other matters related to communication efficiency.

(3) After completing the inspection, the inspectors from the International Radio Station shall immediately fill out four copies of the inspection report: one copy shall be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for verification, one copy shall be sent to the Maritime Affairs Bureau for review, one copy shall be given to the ship captain or their agent for reference, and one copy shall be kept at the station.

(4) If the inspection report contains any deficiencies in the equipment of the ship radio station, the Maritime Affairs Bureau shall urge the ship to promptly organize and improve it.

(5) After the ship radio station has been organized and improved, a written report shall be immediately submitted to the Maritime Affairs Bureau, which shall notify the International Radio Station to send personnel for re-inspection. If any deficiencies are still found, the provisions of Article 4 shall be followed.

Ministry of Communications Actively Organizes Ship Radio Stations 219

Many ship radio stations installed on Chinese merchant ships are poorly equipped, resulting in low communication efficiency, which greatly affects navigation safety. It is now heard that the Ministry of Communications, in order to improve the communication efficiency of various ship radio stations, has stipulated the following organizational measures:

(1) When Chinese merchant ships equipped with ship radio stations arrive in Shanghai, the captain or their agent shall immediately submit a written report to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, which shall notify the Shanghai International Radio Station to dispatch engineers or technicians for inspection.

(2) When technicians from the International Radio Station inspect ship radio stations, they should pay attention to the following points: (1) Whether the transmitting and receiving equipment is well maintained? (2) Whether the power supply equipment is appropriate? (3) Whether the frequency of the transmitter is accurate? (4) Whether the antenna method, height, and length are appropriate? (5) Whether there are spare transmitters and receivers and automatic alarm machines? (6) Whether the batteries are well maintained? (7) Whether the location and equipment of the radio room are appropriate? (8) Whether the radio station and radio operators have licenses; whether the radio operators' skills are excellent? How many radio operators are there in total? (9) Whether the wireless compass is accurate? (10) Other matters related to communication efficiency.

(3) After completing the inspection, the inspectors from the International Radio Station shall immediately fill out four copies of the inspection report: one copy shall be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for verification, one copy shall be sent to the Maritime Affairs Bureau for review, one copy shall be given to the ship captain or their agent for reference, and one copy shall be kept at the station.

(4) If the inspection report contains any deficiencies in the equipment of the ship radio station, the Maritime Affairs Bureau shall urge the ship to promptly organize and improve it.

(5) After the ship radio station has been organized and improved, a written report shall be immediately submitted to the Maritime Affairs Bureau, which shall notify the International Radio Station to send personnel for re-inspection. If any deficiencies are still found, the provisions of Article 4 shall be followed.

Question and Answer Column 220

This publication has specially opened a question and answer column. Members of the public who have questions regarding the procedures for sending and receiving telegrams and telephones, or who are unclear about telecommunications regulations, or who have any inquiries about telecommunications knowledge, are welcome to contact us. We will answer them sincerely.

(1) Mr. Liu Ziqi of Changsha asks: Now that the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Communications have issued orders to implement cash collection for government and military telegrams, should this be followed? However, can the name and address of the recipient be calculated as three characters if they are less than thirteen characters, as with ordinary telegrams?

(Answer) According to the provisions of Article 83 of the General Rules for Domestic Telegram Business, the recipient's address and name for government and military telegrams shall be charged according to the original number of characters. The cost per character of a telegram is consistently above one dime, and the telegraph bureau has already lost half of the fee by halving the fees for government and military telegrams. Therefore, the recipient's address and name are not treated in the same way as ordinary telegrams.

(2) Mr. Liu Chucai of Nanjing asks: I am currently planning to make a long-distance call from Nanjing to a friend in Jiujiang to discuss a certain important matter, and pay at half price according to the government and military telegram rate. Is this possible?

(Answer) According to the General Rules for Long-Distance Telephone Business, there are no provisions for half-price charges. Moreover, the Nanjing-Jiujiang long-distance telephone line is one of the main lines of the long-distance telephone network of nine provinces. The capital for this telephone line project is a loan from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund to the Ministry of Communications. According to the contract, all telephone revenue is the primary guarantee. Tolls must be paid according to regulations, and there is no room for flexibility. It is also heard that the Executive Yuan has issued orders to various political and military agencies to maintain it.

Correction: In the previous issue of this publication, in the article "Completion of the Nanjing-Hankou Trunk Line of the Nine-Province Long-Distance Telephone Network," Nanjing to Huaining and Nanjing to Wuhu, Hankou to Jiujiang and Huaining to Jiujiang are all direct, which was incorrectly published as "via Jiujiang." This is hereby corrected.

Statistics on Accidental Events 221

— Lian

According to the China Daily: "In May of this year, 171 accidental events occurred in the Public Concession due to industrial and occupational reasons, which were reported to the Municipal Council. Among them, 8 were fatal, 8 women were injured, and 1 was fatal. The causes of the accidental events were known in 161 cases. The Municipal Council investigated and ordered the adoption of preventive measures in 107 cases." In this alarming number, the occupations of the deceased and injured are statistically divided, and workers in the metal and machinery industries account for the largest number, with a total of 60 deaths and injuries. There were 27 deaths and injuries among construction workers, 16 deaths and injuries among textile workers, 21 deaths and injuries among transport workers, and 15 deaths and injuries among papermaking and printing workers. … According to an examination of the causes of death and injury, 13 accidental events occurred in gears or belts, 51 occurred in power machines, 11 occurred in pressure machines, and 11 occurred in rolling mills. … And these statistics on accidental events are only within May, and only belong to one corner of the Shanghai Public Concession, and the number is already so alarming. If we extrapolate proportionally, the seriousness can be imagined.

We really cannot ignore these accidental events. From the causes of the accidents, we can at least be sure that the methods of preventing accidents are not very sound, which makes the safety of workers lose its guarantee, and they have to reluctantly do it because they are driven by life. This has led to an increase in the number of accidental events, which is indeed a cruel human tragedy.

From the standpoint of humanity and justice, we cannot remain silent about the protection of workers' lives. Although we also know that in this turbulent era, even if we make improvements, it is still not a thorough solution. We think that sometimes even if we can slightly reduce the severity, it is not unhelpful to make small improvements first.

The suffering of Chinese workers' lives is already greater than that of European and American countries, and the lack of protection of their lives is even more unbearable for people with a sense of humanity and justice. Now, according to the Municipal Council's statistics for May, the number of workers who are frequently injured or killed in accidents is still so large. Then, those who have not been published and those who have not been investigated and counted should be more than this number. Therefore, for the sake of the future of Chinese workers, it is necessary to appeal to the public again and again.

A Tour of Allen Goat Milk Farm 222

— Fang Zhou

Special Report from this Newspaper

Goat milk farms in our country can be said to be an emerging industry; because its discovery was only a year ago. And I only knew that there was a goat milk company on Jiangwan Road in Shanghai at first. Until recently, I went to Zhenru twice, and I realized that there was also an Allen Goat Milk Farm there.

But Chinese people are still very unfamiliar with goat milk, and they don't understand what the difference is between its quality and cow milk, so very few people eat it, and it is difficult to promote it widely for a while. —— The goat milk business in Europe, America, and Japan is almost as developed as the cow milk industry; especially in Sweden, goat milk farms have almost become an important sideline in the countryside. So I always wanted to visit there, and I also wanted to introduce some of the situation inside to the readers in our country who are concerned about the production industry.

Yesterday afternoon, that public bus took me from Baoshan Road to the front of Jinan University in Zhenru; I braved the dust that was rolled up into the air by the bus and walked along that cinder road. On the bridge block, I saw the signposts for Allen Goat Milk Farm and the Zhenru Rural Education Experimental Zone; following the direction of the signposts across the bridge, it was the wide and flat Zhenru Road.

After passing Zhenru Middle School, both sides were full of fields. The melon vines and bean vines in the fields, and the bean pods and cotton seedlings, were all crouching under the scorching sun in a lovely green color. Some flowers were hiding on the green leaves like butterflies. Although there are also a few villa-style foreign houses and a few small plantations or flower gardens along the road, they are as sparse as morning stars.

Some cotton fields have black signs that say "Zhenru Rural Education Experimental Zone Cotton Demonstration Farm," which are special fields for agricultural improvement experiments.

Allen Goat Milk Farm is about a mile away from Zhenru Railway Station and covers an area of ten acres. It is surrounded by bamboo fences. Next to it is a farm office, and opposite it is the general office of the Zhenru Rural Education Experimental Zone.

I went inside, found the office, explained my intention to a female clerk, and she sent a manager to guide me through the visit.

First, I visited the milk bottle disinfection room; there is a bottle washing machine there. All empty bottles prepared for filling milk must first be washed on this machine and then placed in a steam box for disinfection. This kind of steam box is installed in the wall. Each box is divided into six drawers, and each drawer can hold 60 empty bottles. There are six complete steam boxes, and each box is equipped with a thermometer. After putting the washed empty bottles in the box, the door must be closed, and at the same time, the steam in this box is released. The average temperature of the steam is 200 to 220 degrees. —— And this box has doors on both sides, one side is in the bottle washing room, and the other side is in the bottle filling room. When disinfecting, it is put in from here, and when filling milk, it is taken out from there. The procedure can be said to be very convenient.

The milking room is in the back; there are also two rooms here, one is for washing the sheep before milking; after washing the sheep, they are milked in that room. Milking is done manually; they ride the sheep on a wooden frame, and people sit under its belly and slowly squeeze the milk out. After the milk is squeezed out, it must be sent upstairs to the steam pot for disinfection immediately. In addition to a very large steam pot, there is also a circular thermometer on the wall, like a wall clock, and the temperature required for steaming milk is about 140 to 150 degrees. Walking down the cement stairs next to it is the bottle filling room. There is a bottle filling machine here. Above the bottle filling machine is a refrigeration machine. One end of the machine is connected to the milk steaming pot through a pipe, and the other end is connected to the funnel of the bottle filling machine. On the wall is the steam box door for milk bottle disinfection. Behind is a cold room. After the goat milk is filled into bottles, it is stored in the cold room.

After visiting these places, we went to visit the sheep pen; there are two houses in the sheep pen. Each house has two rows of iron railings and two troughs. Each sheep lives separately and cannot compete for food or invade territory. And the house must be washed once every day, so it is very clean; and they must be grazed in the outside garden once every day.

The capital for the opening of the farm is 100,000 yuan, and there are currently more than 200 sheep. These sheep are all Swedish breeds, and each one is worth about 80 yuan. On average, one sheep can be milked twice a day, at least 8 pounds. If no accidents occur, one sheep can produce milk for three years. After three years, it will not be able to produce milk. The udders of these sheep are very large, and they look a bit like the udders of cows.

Their feed is similar to that of sheep, consisting of soybeans, wheat, soybean cakes, and grass, etc., but their wool and meat are insufficient for use in addition to producing milk.

As for the difference between goat milk and cow milk, goat milk has less T.B, but other proteins and vitamins are the same, and goat milk is better than cow milk, because cow milk is hot in nature and is not suitable for people who are sick or weak or have stomach problems. Goat milk is very beneficial to people with stomach problems, and it does not matter whether it is cold or warm in season.

In terms of price, there is not much difference between goat milk and cow milk.

However, it is necessary to manage these sheep well, such as the cleanliness of the houses, the circulation of air, and the prevention of diseases, all of which require strict equipment. Otherwise, there is inevitably a danger of death and infection from time to time!

It has only been open for more than a year now, but it is said that the results are very good, and the sales of milk are not bad, but these sales are all in Shanghai, and there are very few elsewhere.

Finally, I toured all parts of the farm; there. In addition to the sheep pen and the various parts of the bottle filling area, there is also an office, a relay office, a self-flowing well motor room and a water storage pavilion, a cement room, and a thatched pavilion on the lawn in front. Moreover, this place is full of rural flavor. Not only is the environment quiet, the air is fresh, and the scenery is even more beautiful, but the transportation is also very convenient, so I think this location is really too good.

Laughter and Tears — Quick Sketches from the Slanted Bridge 223

—

Automobile 224

— Zhi Min

Mrs. Zhu seemed to be angry with someone. I already heard the sound of high-heeled leather shoes when she entered the door. Today is the wedding of one of her classmates. A week ago, she prepared diligently for herself and her husband, and she was very happy to have such an opportunity to boast to her many classmates that her husband was such an honest and handsome man. But it happened to be the time for the bank's closing accounts, and she couldn't ask for leave in the bank. Mr. Zhu loved his wife very much. He knew that his wife's efforts for the week had been in vain, so he said to his wife apologetically the next evening:

"There's nothing I can do about it. After eating other people's food, I can't ask for leave during these two periods of the year; but I'll try to get out earlier and have dinner there, wouldn't that be the same?"

But when Mr. Zhu came out of the bank today, it was already ten o'clock in the evening. He expected that the guests would be leaving soon.

Mrs. Zhu felt that it was an insult, and an insult to her husband. But when she told those classmates,
